EventTargetChainItem.\n   */\n  uint16_t mItemFlags;\n\n  /**\n   * Data for items in the event target chain.\n   * Set in GetEventTargetParent() and used in PostHandleEvent().\n   *\n   * @note This data is different for each item in the event target chain.\n   *       It is up to the Pre/PostHandleEvent implementation to decide how to\n   *       use this.\n   */\n  nsCOMPtr<nsISupports> mParentTarget = aParentTarget;\n    if (mParentTarget) {\n      mParentIsChromeHandler = aIsChromeHandler;\n    }\n  }\n\n  void IgnoreCurrentTargetBecauseOfShadowDOMRetargeting();\n\n  /**\n   * dispatch system follows the W3C DOM specification for event flow, implementing capture, target, and bubble phases. The dispatch chain begins in `EventDispatcher::Dispatch()` and involves multiple components working together to propagate events through the DOM tree and invoke listeners.\\n\\n## Key Components and Flow\\n\\n### 1. Event Creation\\n**File: `dom/events/Event.cpp` and `dom/events/Event.h`**\\n- The `Event` class constructor (Event.cpp) creates DOM Event objects that wrap WidgetEvent instances\\n- Events are created on-demand during dispatch or can be provided by callers\\n- Each Event holds reference to its original target, current target, and related targets\\n\\n### 2. Event Dispatch Entry Point\\n**File: `dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp` (line 869)**\\n- **Function: `EventDispatcher::Dispatch()`** - The main entry point for event dispatching\\n  - Takes an initial target, WidgetEvent, and optional DOM Event\\n  - Sets up the event for dispatch and creates the event target chain\\n  - Handles retargeting for native anonymous content and chrome dispatch\\n  - Manages event status and default prevention\\n  - Calls `EventDispatcher::DispatchDOMEvent()` for DOM Event dispatching\\n\\n### 3. Event Target Chain Creation\\n**File: `dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp`**\\n- **Class: `EventTargetChainItem`** - Represents a single item in the event target chain\\n  - Created by `EventTargetChainItem::Create()` which builds a singly-linked chain\\n  - Caches flags (mForceContentDispatch, mWantsWillHandleEvent, mMayHaveListenerManager, etc.)\\n  - Stores retargeted related targets and touch targets for proper event path construction\\n  \\n- **Function: `EventTargetChainItem::GetEventTargetParent()`** - Chain construction\\n  - Calls `mTarget->GetEventTargetParent(aVisitor)` on each target\\n  - Collects parent target information to build the chain\\n  - Handles retargeting for Shadow DOM and anonymous content boundaries\\n  - Sets flags indicating whether the target wants pre/post event handling\\n\\n- **Virtual Method: `EventTarget::GetEventTargetParent()`** (dom/events/EventTarget.h:282)\\n  - Implemented by specific event targets (Element, Document, Window, etc.)\\n  - Sets `aVisitor.mParentTarget` to indicate the next target in the chain\\n  - Sets `aVisitor.mCanHandle = false` to stop chain construction if needed\\n  - Handles retargeting of related targets and touch targets for Shadow DOM\\n\\n### 4.
